SYSTEM: You are a helpful assistant.

USER: i want to build a go program that basically serves a mostly static website. the website will present and allow to search for videos. videos are all in subdirectories, very mixed formats, but let's assume for now that they will all work in a HTML video player and do not need transcoding. the program will build a database if not yet present, or have a flag that will trigger an update (mostly new videos, probably some deletions) with some video metadata - notably video length, path and filename, and allows for augmenting this with a tagging system. maybe identify video files by a hash instead of path/filename. might be sufficient to work on the first, say five minutes, or 10 mbyte or so for the hashing. i'm thinking of some simple bolt based database maybe. search features for tags of course, and edit features for tags. search features for filename and path. fast tagging of multiple videos. per video thumbnails, and a automatic flip-though through about 10-20 thumbnails per video as a mouse-over effect. video list presentation in a tabular style that adopts to screen size. maybe later some "similar videos" system based on tags, presenting under the video player.

ASSISTANT: 

# Video Library Server - Design & Implementation

This is a substantial project. I'll build it incrementally with a solid foundation.

## models/models.go

```go
package models

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"time"
)

// Video represents a video file in the library
type Video struct {
	Hash         string    `json:"hash"`          // partial-content hash (first 10MB)
	Path         string    `json:"path"`          // full path to file
	Filename     string    `json:"filename"`      // just the filename
	Directory    string    `json:"directory"`      // parent directory
	Size         int64     `json:"size"`          // file size in bytes
	Duration     float64   `json:"duration"`      // duration in seconds
	Width        int       `json:"width"`         // video width
	Height       int       `json:"height"`        // video height
	Tags         []string  `json:"tags"`          // user-assigned tags
	ThumbnailDir string    `json:"thumbnail_dir"` // path to thumbnail directory
	ThumbCount   int       `json:"thumb_count"`   // number of generated thumbnails
	AddedAt      time.Time `json:"added_at"`
	ModifiedAt   time.Time `json:"modified_at"`
	FileModTime  time.Time `json:"file_mod_time"`
}

func (v *Video) Marshal() ([]byte, error) {
	return json.Marshal(v)
}

func UnmarshalVideo(data []byte) (*Video, error) {
	var v Video
	err := json.Unmarshal(data, &v)
	return &v, err
}

// DurationString returns a human-readable duration
func (v *Video) DurationString() string {
	d := time.Duration(v.Duration * float64(time.Second))
	h := int(d.Hours())
	m := int(d.Minutes()) % 60
	s := int(d.Seconds()) % 60
	if h > 0 {
		return fmt.Sprintf("%d:%02d:%02d", h, m, s)
	}
	return fmt.Sprintf("%d:%02d", m, s)
}

// SizeString returns a human-readable file size
func (v *Video) SizeString() string {
	const (
		MB = 1024 * 1024
		GB = 1024 * MB
	)
	switch {
	case v.Size >= GB:
		return fmt.Sprintf("%.1f GB", float64(v.Size)/float64(GB))
	case v.Size >= MB:
		return fmt.Sprintf("%.1f MB", float64(v.Size)/float64(MB))
	default:
		return fmt.Sprintf("%d KB", v.Size/1024)
	}
}

// SearchResult wraps a video with search relevance info
type SearchResult struct {
	Video      *Video  `json:"video"`
	Relevance  float64 `json:"relevance"`
}

// TagInfo holds tag usage statistics
type TagInfo struct {
	Name  string `json:"name"`
	Count int    `json:"count"`
}
```

Fix the models package (it needs fmt import):

```go
package models

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"time"
)

// Video represents a video file in the library
type Video struct {
	Hash         string    `json:"hash"`
	Path         string    `json:"path"`
	Filename     string    `json:"filename"`
	Directory    string    `json:"directory"`
	Size         int64     `json:"size"`
	Duration     float64   `json:"duration"`
	Width        int       `json:"width"`
	Height       int       `json:"height"`
	Tags         []string  `json:"tags"`
	ThumbnailDir string    `json:"thumbnail_dir"`
	ThumbCount   int       `json:"thumb_count"`
	AddedAt      time.Time `json:"added_at"`
	ModifiedAt   time.Time `json:"modified_at"`
	FileModTime  time.Time `json:"file_mod_time"`
}

func (v *Video) Marshal() ([]byte, error) {
	return json.Marshal(v)
}

func UnmarshalVideo(data []byte) (*Video, error) {
	var v Video
	err := json.Unmarshal(data, &v)
	return &v, err
}

func (v *Video) DurationString() string {
	d := time.Duration(v.Duration * float64(time.Second))
	h := int(d.Hours())
	m := int(d.Minutes()) % 60
	s := int(d.Seconds()) % 60
	if h > 0 {
		return fmt.Sprintf("%d:%02d:%02d", h, m, s)
	}
	return fmt.Sprintf("%d:%02d", m, s)
}

func (v *Video) SizeString() string {
	const (
		MB = 1024 * 1024
		GB = 1024 * MB
	)
	switch {
	case v.Size >= GB:
		return fmt.Sprintf("%.1f GB", float64(v.Size)/float64(GB))
	case v.Size >= MB:
		return fmt.Sprintf("%.1f MB", float64(v.Size)/float64(MB))
	default:
		return fmt.Sprintf("%d KB", v.Size/1024)
	}
}

	Name  string `json:"name"`
```

## hasher/hasher.go

```go
package hasher

import (
	"crypto/sha256"
	"encoding/hex"
	"io"
	"os"
)

const (
	// HashSize is the number of bytes to read for partial hashing
	// 10 MB should be enough to uniquely identify most video files
	HashSize = 10 * 1024 * 1024
)

// HashFile computes a SHA-256 hash of the first HashSize bytes of a file.
// For files smaller than HashSize, the entire file is hashed.
// The file size is mixed into the hash to differentiate files that share
// identical first 10MB but differ in length.
func HashFile(path string) (string, error) {
	f, err := os.Open(path)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	defer f.Close()

	// Get file size to mix into hash
	stat, err := f.Stat()
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}

	h := sha256.New()

	// Write file size as 8 bytes (big-endian) into hash
	size := stat.Size()
	sizeBytes := make([]byte, 8)
	for i := 7; i >= 0; i-- {
		sizeBytes[i] = byte(size & 0xff)
		size >>= 8
	}
	h.Write(sizeBytes)

	// Read up to HashSize bytes
	reader := io.LimitReader(f, HashSize)
	if _, err := io.Copy(h, reader); err != nil {
		return "", err
	}

	return hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil)), nil
}
```

## db/database.go

```go
package db

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"sort"
	"strings"
	"time"

	"videolib/models"

	bolt "go.etcd.io/bbolt"
)

var (
	// Bucket names
	videoBucket    = []byte("videos")     // hash -> Video JSON
	pathBucket     = []byte("paths")      // filepath -> hash (index)
	tagBucket      = []byte("tags")       // tag -> JSON array of hashes
	metaBucket     = []byte("meta")       // metadata (scan times, etc.)
)

type Database struct {
	db *bolt.DB
}

func Open(path string) (*Database, error) {
	bdb, err := bolt.Open(path, 0600, &bolt.Options{Timeout: 1 * time.Second})
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("opening database: %w", err)
	}

	// Ensure all buckets exist
	err = bdb.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		for _, bucket := range [][]byte{videoBucket, pathBucket, tagBucket, metaBucket} {
			if _, err := tx.CreateBucketIfNotExists(bucket); err != nil {
				return err
			}
		}
		return nil
	})
	if err != nil {
		bdb.Close()
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("initializing buckets: %w", err)
	}

	return &Database{db: bdb}, nil
}

func (d *Database) Close() error {
	return d.db.Close()
}

// PutVideo stores or updates a video record
func (d *Database) PutVideo(v *models.Video) error {
	return d.db.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		data, err := v.Marshal()
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		// Store video by hash
		if err := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Put([]byte(v.Hash), data); err != nil {
			return err
		}

		// Update path index
		if err := tx.Bucket(pathBucket).Put([]byte(v.Path), []byte(v.Hash)); err != nil {
			return err
		}

		// Update tag indices
		for _, tag := range v.Tags {
			if err := d.addHashToTag(tx, tag, v.Hash); err != nil {
				return err
			}
		}

		return nil
	})
}

// GetVideo retrieves a video by its hash
func (d *Database) GetVideo(hash string) (*models.Video, error) {
	var video *models.Video
	err := d.db.View(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
		if data == nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("video not found: %s", hash)
		}
		var err error
		video, err = models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
		return err
	})
	return video, err
}

// GetVideoByPath retrieves a video by its file path
func (d *Database) GetVideoByPath(path string) (*models.Video, error) {
	var video *models.Video
	err := d.db.View(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		hash := tx.Bucket(pathBucket).Get([]byte(path))
		if hash == nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("video not found at path: %s", path)
		}
		data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get(hash)
		if data == nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("video data missing for hash: %s", string(hash))
		}
		var err error
		video, err = models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
		return err
	})
	return video, err
}

// DeleteVideo removes a video and cleans up indices
func (d *Database) DeleteVideo(hash string) error {
	return d.db.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		// Get the video first to clean up indices
		data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
		if data == nil {
			return nil // Already gone
		}

		video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		// Remove from path index
		tx.Bucket(pathBucket).Delete([]byte(video.Path))

		// Remove from tag indices
		for _, tag := range video.Tags {
			d.removeHashFromTag(tx, tag, hash)
		}

		// Remove video record
		return tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Delete([]byte(hash))
	})
}

// ListAllVideos returns all videos in the database
func (d *Database) ListAllVideos() ([]*models.Video, error) {
	var videos []*models.Video
	err := d.db.View(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		return tx.Bucket(videoBucket).ForEach(func(k, v []byte) error {
			video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(v)
			if err != nil {
				return err
			}
			videos = append(videos, video)
			return nil
		})
	})
	return videos, err
}

// SearchByFilename searches videos by filename substring (case-insensitive)
func (d *Database) SearchByFilename(query string) ([]*models.Video, error) {
	query = strings.ToLower(query)
	var results []*models.Video
	err := d.db.View(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		return tx.Bucket(videoBucket).ForEach(func(k, v []byte) error {
			video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(v)
			if err != nil {
				return err
			}
			if strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(video.Filename), query) ||
				strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(video.Path), query) {
				results = append(results, video)
			}
			return nil
		})
	})
	return results, err
}

// SearchByTags returns videos that have ALL of the specified tags
func (d *Database) SearchByTags(tags []string) ([]*models.Video, error) {
	if len(tags) == 0 {
		return d.ListAllVideos()
	}

	var results []*models.Video
	err := d.db.View(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		// Get hash sets for each tag
		var hashSets []map[string]bool
		for _, tag := range tags {
			hashes, err := d.getTagHashes(tx, strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(tag)))
			if err != nil {
				return err
			}
			set := make(map[string]bool)
			for _, h := range hashes {
				set[h] = true
			}
			hashSets = append(hashSets, set)
		}

		if len(hashSets) == 0 {
			return nil
		}

		// Intersect all sets
		intersection := hashSets[0]
		for i := 1; i < len(hashSets); i++ {
			newIntersection := make(map[string]bool)
			for h := range intersection {
				if hashSets[i][h] {
					newIntersection[h] = true
				}
			}
			intersection = newIntersection
		}

		// Fetch videos
		for hash := range intersection {
			data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
			if data != nil {
				video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
				if err == nil {
					results = append(results, video)
				}
			}
		}
		return nil
	})
	return results, err
}

// SetTags replaces all tags on a video
func (d *Database) SetTags(hash string, tags []string) error {
	return d.db.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
		if data == nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("video not found: %s", hash)
		}

		video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		// Remove from old tag indices
		for _, oldTag := range video.Tags {
			d.removeHashFromTag(tx, oldTag, hash)
		}

		// Normalize and deduplicate tags
		normalized := make([]string, 0, len(tags))
		seen := make(map[string]bool)
		for _, t := range tags {
			t = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(t))
			if t != "" && !seen[t] {
				normalized = append(normalized, t)
				seen[t] = true
			}
		}
		sort.Strings(normalized)

		video.Tags = normalized
		video.ModifiedAt = time.Now()

		// Add to new tag indices
		for _, tag := range normalized {
			if err := d.addHashToTag(tx, tag, hash); err != nil {
				return err
			}
		}

		// Save updated video
		newData, err := video.Marshal()
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		return tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Put([]byte(hash), newData)
	})
}

// AddTags adds tags to a video (keeps existing)
func (d *Database) AddTags(hash string, tags []string) error {
	return d.db.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
		if data == nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("video not found: %s", hash)
		}

		video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		existing := make(map[string]bool)
		for _, t := range video.Tags {
			existing[t] = true
		}

		for _, t := range tags {
			t = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(t))
			if t != "" && !existing[t] {
				video.Tags = append(video.Tags, t)
				existing[t] = true
				if err := d.addHashToTag(tx, t, hash); err != nil {
					return err
				}
			}
		}

		sort.Strings(video.Tags)
		video.ModifiedAt = time.Now()

		newData, err := video.Marshal()
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		return tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Put([]byte(hash), newData)
	})
}

// RemoveTags removes specific tags from a video
func (d *Database) RemoveTags(hash string, tags []string) error {
	return d.db.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
		if data == nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("video not found: %s", hash)
		}

		video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		toRemove := make(map[string]bool)
		for _, t := range tags {
			t = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(t))
			toRemove[t] = true
		}

		newTags := make([]string, 0)
		for _, t := range video.Tags {
			if toRemove[t] {
				d.removeHashFromTag(tx, t, hash)
			} else {
				newTags = append(newTags, t)
			}
		}

		video.Tags = newTags
		video.ModifiedAt = time.Now()

		newData, err := video.Marshal()
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		return tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Put([]byte(hash), newData)
	})
}

// BulkAddTags adds tags to multiple videos at once
func (d *Database) BulkAddTags(hashes []string, tags []string) error {
	return d.db.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		for _, hash := range hashes {
			data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
			if data == nil {
				continue
			}

			video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
			if err != nil {
				continue
			}

			existing := make(map[string]bool)
			for _, t := range video.Tags {
				existing[t] = true
			}

			changed := false
			for _, t := range tags {
				t = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(t))
				if t != "" && !existing[t] {
					video.Tags = append(video.Tags, t)
					existing[t] = true
					d.addHashToTag(tx, t, hash)
					changed = true
				}
			}

			if changed {
				sort.Strings(video.Tags)
				video.ModifiedAt = time.Now()
				newData, _ := video.Marshal()
				tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Put([]byte(hash), newData)
			}
		}
		return nil
	})
}

// BulkRemoveTags removes tags from multiple videos at once
func (d *Database) BulkRemoveTags(hashes []string, tags []string) error {
	return d.db.Update(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		toRemove := make(map[string]bool)
		for _, t := range tags {
			toRemove[strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(t))] = true
		}

		for _, hash := range hashes {
			data := tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Get([]byte(hash))
			if data == nil {
				continue
			}
			video, err := models.UnmarshalVideo(data)
			if err != nil {
				continue
			}

			newTags := make([]string, 0)
			changed := false
			for _, t := range video.Tags {
				if toRemove[t] {
					d.removeHashFromTag(tx, t, hash)
					changed = true
				} else {
					newTags = append(newTags, t)
				}
			}

			if changed {
				video.Tags = newTags
				video.ModifiedAt = time.Now()
				newData, _ := video.Marshal()
				tx.Bucket(videoBucket).Put([]byte(hash), newData)
			}
		}
		return nil
	})
}

// ListAllTags returns all tags with usage counts
func (d *Database) ListAllTags() ([]models.TagInfo, error) {
	var tags []models.TagInfo
	err := d.db.View(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		return tx.Bucket(tagBucket).ForEach(func(k, v []byte) error {
			var hashes []string
			if err := json.Unmarshal(v, &hashes); err != nil {
				return nil // skip malformed
			}
			if len(hashes) > 0 {
				tags = append(tags, models.TagInfo{
					Name:  string(k),
					Count: len(hashes),
				})
			}
			return nil
		})
	})
	sort.Slice(tags, func(i, j int) bool {
		return tags[i].Name < tags[j].Name
	})
	return tags, err
}

// GetAllPaths returns all known file paths (for scan comparison)
func (d *Database) GetAllPaths() (map[string]string, error) {
	paths := make(map[string]string)
	err := d.db.View(func(tx *bolt.Tx) error {
		return tx.Bucket(pathBucket).ForEach(func(k, v []byte) error {
			paths[string(k)] = string(v)
			return nil
		})
	})
	return paths, err
}

// --- internal helpers ---

func (d *Database) addHashToTag(tx *bolt.Tx, tag, hash string) error {
	hashes, _ := d.getTagHashes(tx, tag)
	for _, h := range hashes {
		if h == hash {
			return nil // already present
		}
	}
	hashes = append(hashes, hash)
	data, err := json.Marshal(hashes)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	return tx.Bucket(tagBucket).Put([]byte(tag), data)
}

func (d *Database) removeHashFromTag(tx *bolt.Tx, tag, hash string) {
	hashes, _ := d.getTagHashes(tx, tag)
	newHashes := make([]string, 0, len(hashes))
	for _, h := range hashes {
		if h != hash {
			newHashes = append(newHashes, h)
		}
	}
	if len(newHashes) == 0 {
		tx.Bucket(tagBucket).Delete([]byte(tag))
	} else {
		data, _ := json.Marshal(newHashes)
		tx.Bucket(tagBucket).Put([]byte(tag), data)
	}
}

func (d *Database) getTagHashes(tx *bolt.Tx, tag string) ([]string, error) {
	data := tx.Bucket(tagBucket).Get([]byte(tag))
	if data == nil {
		return nil, nil
	}
	var hashes []string
	err := json.Unmarshal(data, &hashes)
	return hashes, err
}
```

## scanner/scanner.go

```go
package scanner

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"os"
	"os/exec"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"time"

	"videolib/db"
	"videolib/hasher"
	"videolib/models"
)

var videoExtensions = map[string]bool{
	".mp4":  true,
	".mkv":  true,
	".avi":  true,
	".mov":  true,
	".wmv":  true,
	".flv":  true,
	".webm": true,
	".m4v":  true,
	".mpg":  true,
	".mpeg": true,
	".3gp":  true,
	".ogv":  true,
	".ts":   true,
	".vob":  true,
	".divx": true,
	".rm":   true,
	".rmvb": true,
}

type Scanner struct {
	database     *db.Database
	roots        []string
	thumbDir     string
	thumbCount   int
	workers      int
}

type ScanResult struct {
	Added   int
	Removed int
	Errors  int
	Total   int
}

func New(database *db.Database, roots []string, thumbDir string) *Scanner {
	return &Scanner{
		database:   database,
		roots:      roots,
		thumbDir:   thumbDir,
		thumbCount: 16,
		workers:    4,
	}
}

func (s *Scanner) Scan() (*ScanResult, error) {
	result := &ScanResult{}

	// Collect all video files on disk
	log.Println("Scanning directories for video files...")
	diskFiles := make(map[string]os.FileInfo)
	for _, root := range s.roots {
		err := filepath.Walk(root, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
			if err != nil {
				log.Printf("Warning: cannot access %s: %v", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			if info.IsDir() {
				return nil
			}
			ext := strings.ToLower(filepath.Ext(path))
			if videoExtensions[ext] {
				absPath, err := filepath.Abs(path)
				if err != nil {
					return nil
				}
				diskFiles[absPath] = info
			}
			return nil
		})
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("scanning %s: %w", root, err)
		}
	}
	log.Printf("Found %d video files on disk", len(diskFiles))
	result.Total = len(diskFiles)

	// Get existing database paths
	existingPaths, err := s.database.GetAllPaths()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("reading existing paths: %w", err)
	}

	// Find deleted files
	for path, hash := range existingPaths {
		if _, exists := diskFiles[path]; !exists {
			log.Printf("Removing deleted file: %s", path)
			if err := s.database.DeleteVideo(hash); err != nil {
				log.Printf("Error removing %s: %v", path, err)
				result.Errors++
			} else {
				result.Removed++
			}
		}
	}

	// Find new/modified files
	type workItem struct {
		path string
		info os.FileInfo
	}

	items := make([]workItem, 0)
	for path, info := range diskFiles {
		if _, exists := existingPaths[path]; !exists {
			items = append(items, workItem{path, info})
		}
		// TODO: could also check mod time for changes
	}

	log.Printf("Processing %d new files...", len(items))

	for i, item := range items {
		log.Printf("[%d/%d] Processing: %s", i+1, len(items), item.path)

		video, err := s.processFile(item.path, item.info)
		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("Error processing %s: %v", item.path, err)
			result.Errors++
			continue
		}

		if err := s.database.PutVideo(video); err != nil {
			log.Printf("Error storing %s: %v", item.path, err)
			result.Errors++
			continue
		}

		// Generate thumbnails
		if err := s.generateThumbnails(video); err != nil {
			log.Printf("Warning: thumbnail generation failed for %s: %v", item.path, err)
			// Not a fatal error
		}

		result.Added++
	}

	return result, nil
}

func (s *Scanner) processFile(path string, info os.FileInfo) (*models.Video, error) {
	// Hash the file
	hash, err := hasher.HashFile(path)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("hashing: %w", err)
	}

	// Probe video metadata with ffprobe
	duration, width, height := s.probeVideo(path)

	video := &models.Video{
		Hash:        hash,
		Path:        path,
		Filename:    filepath.Base(path),
		Directory:   filepath.Dir(path),
		Size:        info.Size(),
		Duration:    duration,
		Width:       width,
		Height:      height,
		Tags:        []string{},
		ThumbCount:  0,
		AddedAt:     time.Now(),
		ModifiedAt:  time.Now(),
		FileModTime: info.ModTime(),
	}

	return video, nil
}

// ffprobeResult is the JSON structure returned by ffprobe
type ffprobeResult struct {
	Format struct {
		Duration string `json:"duration"`
	} `json:"format"`
	Streams []struct {
		CodecType string `json:"codec_type"`
		Width     int    `json:"width"`
		Height    int    `json:"height"`
	} `json:"streams"`
}

func (s *Scanner) probeVideo(path string) (duration float64, width, height int) {
	cmd := exec.Command("ffprobe",
		"-v", "quiet",
		"-print_format", "json",
		"-show_format",
		"-show_streams",
		path,
	)

	output, err := cmd.Output()
	if err != nil {
		log.Printf("ffprobe failed for %s: %v", path, err)
		return 0, 0, 0
	}

	var result ffprobeResult
	if err := json.Unmarshal(output, &result); err != nil {
		log.Printf("ffprobe parse failed for %s: %v", path, err)
		return 0, 0, 0
	}

	duration, _ = strconv.ParseFloat(result.Format.Duration, 64)

	for _, stream := range result.Streams {
		if stream.CodecType == "video" {
			width = stream.Width
			height = stream.Height
			break
		}
	}

	return duration, width, height
}

func (s *Scanner) generateThumbnails(video *models.Video) error {
	if video.Duration <= 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("unknown duration, cannot generate thumbnails")
	}

	thumbDir := filepath.Join(s.thumbDir, video.Hash)
	if err := os.MkdirAll(thumbDir, 0755); err != nil {
		return err
	}

	count := s.thumbCount
	interval := video.Duration / float64(count+1)

	for i := 0; i < count; i++ {
		timestamp := interval * float64(i+1)
		outPath := filepath.Join(thumbDir, fmt.Sprintf("thumb_%02d.jpg", i))

		// Skip if already exists
		if _, err := os.Stat(outPath); err == nil {
			continue
		}

		cmd := exec.Command("ffmpeg",
			"-ss", fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", timestamp),
			"-i", video.Path,
			"-vframes", "1",
			"-vf", "scale=320:-1",
			"-q:v", "5",
			"-y",
			outPath,
		)

		if err := cmd.Run(); err != nil {
			log.Printf("Thumbnail %d failed for %s: %v", i, video.Path, err)
			continue
		}
	}

	// Count actual thumbnails generated
	entries, _ := os.ReadDir(thumbDir)
	video.ThumbnailDir = thumbDir
	video.ThumbCount = len(entries)

	// Update the video record with thumbnail info
	return s.database.PutVideo(video)
}

// RegenerateThumbnails regenerates thumbnails for a specific video
func (s *Scanner) RegenerateThumbnails(hash string) error {
	video, err := s.database.GetVideo(hash)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	return s.generateThumbnails(video)
}
```

## handlers/api.go

```go
package handlers

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"strings"

	"videolib/db"
)

type APIHandler struct {
	DB *db.Database
}

func NewAPIHandler(database *db.Database) *APIHandler {
	return &APIHandler{DB: database}
}

// JSON helper
func writeJSON(w http.ResponseWriter, status int, data interface{}) {
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
	w.WriteHeader(status)
	json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(data)
}

func writeError(w http.ResponseWriter, status int, msg string) {
	writeJSON(w, status, map[string]string{"error": msg})
}

// GET /api/videos - list all or search
func (h *APIHandler) ListVideos(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	query := r.URL.Query().Get("q")
	tagsParam := r.URL.Query().Get("tags")

	if tagsParam != "" {
		tags := strings.Split(tagsParam, ",")
		for i := range tags {
			tags[i] = strings.TrimSpace(tags[i])
		}
		videos, err := h.DB.SearchByTags(tags)
		if err != nil {
			writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
			return
		}
		writeJSON(w, 200, videos)
		return
	}

	if query != "" {
		videos, err := h.DB.SearchByFilename(query)
		if err != nil {
			writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
			return
		}
		writeJSON(w, 200, videos)
		return
	}

	videos, err := h.DB.ListAllVideos()
	if err != nil {
		writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
		return
	}
	writeJSON(w, 200, videos)
}

// GET /api/videos/{hash}
func (h *APIHandler) GetVideo(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" {
		writeError(w, 400, "missing hash")
		return
	}

	video, err := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	if err != nil {
		writeError(w, 404, err.Error())
		return
	}
	writeJSON(w, 200, video)
}

// POST /api/videos/{hash}/tags
// Body: {"tags": ["tag1", "tag2"]}
func (h *APIHandler) AddTags(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" {
		writeError(w, 400, "missing hash")
		return
	}

	var body struct {
		Tags []string `json:"tags"`
	}
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&body); err != nil {
		writeError(w, 400, "invalid JSON")
		return
	}

	if err := h.DB.AddTags(hash, body.Tags); err != nil {
		writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
		return
	}

	video, _ := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	writeJSON(w, 200, video)
}

// PUT /api/videos/{hash}/tags
// Body: {"tags": ["tag1", "tag2"]}
func (h *APIHandler) SetTags(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" {
		writeError(w, 400, "missing hash")
		return
	}

	var body struct {
		Tags []string `json:"tags"`
	}
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&body); err != nil {
		writeError(w, 400, "invalid JSON")
		return
	}

	if err := h.DB.SetTags(hash, body.Tags); err != nil {
		writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
		return
	}

	video, _ := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	writeJSON(w, 200, video)
}

// DELETE /api/videos/{hash}/tags
// Body: {"tags": ["tag1"]}
func (h *APIHandler) RemoveTags(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" {
		writeError(w, 400, "missing hash")
		return
	}

	var body struct {
		Tags []string `json:"tags"`
	}
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&body); err != nil {
		writeError(w, 400, "invalid JSON")
		return
	}

	if err := h.DB.RemoveTags(hash, body.Tags); err != nil {
		writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
		return
	}

	video, _ := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	writeJSON(w, 200, video)
}

// POST /api/bulk/tags
// Body: {"hashes": ["hash1","hash2"], "tags": ["tag1"], "action": "add"|"remove"}
func (h *APIHandler) BulkTags(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	var body struct {
		Hashes []string `json:"hashes"`
		Tags   []string `json:"tags"`
		Action string   `json:"action"`
	}
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&body); err != nil {
		writeError(w, 400, "invalid JSON")
		return
	}

	log.Printf("Bulk tag %s: %d videos, tags: %v", body.Action, len(body.Hashes), body.Tags)

	var err error
	switch body.Action {
	case "add":
		err = h.DB.BulkAddTags(body.Hashes, body.Tags)
	case "remove":
		err = h.DB.BulkRemoveTags(body.Hashes, body.Tags)
	default:
		writeError(w, 400, "action must be 'add' or 'remove'")
		return
	}

	if err != nil {
		writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
		return
	}

	writeJSON(w, 200, map[string]string{"status": "ok"})
}

// GET /api/tags
func (h *APIHandler) ListTags(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	tags, err := h.DB.ListAllTags()
	if err != nil {
		writeError(w, 500, err.Error())
		return
	}
	writeJSON(w, 200, tags)
}
```

## handlers/pages.go

```go
package handlers

import (
	"html/template"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"path/filepath"

	"videolib/db"
)

type PageHandler struct {
	DB        *db.Database
	Templates *template.Template
}

func NewPageHandler(database *db.Database, templateDir string) (*PageHandler, error) {
	// Custom template functions
	funcMap := template.FuncMap{
		"join": func(s []string, sep string) string {
			result := ""
			for i, v := range s {
				if i > 0 {
					result += sep
				}
				result += v
			}
			return result
		},
	}

	tmpl, err := template.New("").Funcs(funcMap).ParseGlob(filepath.Join(templateDir, "*.html"))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	return &PageHandler{
		DB:        database,
		Templates: tmpl,
	}, nil
}

func (h *PageHandler) render(w http.ResponseWriter, name string, data interface{}) {
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/html; charset=utf-8")
	if err := h.Templates.ExecuteTemplate(w, name, data); err != nil {
		log.Printf("Template error: %v", err)
		http.Error(w, "Template error", 500)
	}
}

// GET / - main video listing page
func (h *PageHandler) Index(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.URL.Path != "/" {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}
	h.render(w, "index.html", nil)
}

// GET /video/{hash} - single video view
func (h *PageHandler) VideoPage(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	video, err := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	if err != nil {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}
	h.render(w, "video.html", video)
}

// GET /tags - tag management page
func (h *PageHandler) TagsPage(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	h.render(w, "tags.html", nil)
}
```

## handlers/static.go

```go
package handlers

import (
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"
)

// VideoFileHandler serves the actual video files.
// It maps /media/{hash} to the actual file path from the database.
type VideoFileHandler struct {
	DB *db.Database
}

func NewVideoFileHandler(database *db.Database) *VideoFileHandler {
	return &VideoFileHandler{DB: database}
}

func (h *VideoFileHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	video, err := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	if err != nil {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	// Verify file still exists
	if _, err := os.Stat(video.Path); os.IsNotExist(err) {
		http.Error(w, "Video file not found on disk", 404)
		return
	}

	// Set content type based on extension
	ext := strings.ToLower(filepath.Ext(video.Path))
	contentTypes := map[string]string{
		".mp4":  "video/mp4",
		".webm": "video/webm",
		".ogv":  "video/ogg",
		".mkv":  "video/x-matroska",
		".avi":  "video/x-msvideo",
		".mov":  "video/quicktime",
		".wmv":  "video/x-ms-wmv",
		".flv":  "video/x-flv",
		".m4v":  "video/mp4",
		".ts":   "video/mp2t",
	}
	if ct, ok := contentTypes[ext]; ok {
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", ct)
	}

	// Use ServeFile for proper range request support (seeking)
	http.ServeFile(w, r, video.Path)
}

// ThumbHandler serves thumbnail images
// /thumbs/{hash}/{filename}
type ThumbHandler struct {
	ThumbDir string
}

func NewThumbHandler(thumbDir string) *ThumbHandler {
	return &ThumbHandler{ThumbDir: thumbDir}
}

func (h *ThumbHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	filename := r.PathValue("filename")

	if hash == "" || filename == "" {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	// Sanitize to prevent path traversal
	if strings.Contains(hash, "..") || strings.Contains(filename, "..") {
		http.Error(w, "Invalid path", 400)
		return
	}

	path := filepath.Join(h.ThumbDir, hash, filename)
	if _, err := os.Stat(path); os.IsNotExist(err) {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	w.Header().Set("Cache-Control", "public, max-age=86400")
	http.ServeFile(w, r, path)
}

// ThumbListHandler returns the list of thumbnail filenames for a video
// GET /api/thumbs/{hash}
type ThumbListHandler struct {
	ThumbDir string
}

func (h *ThumbListHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" || strings.Contains(hash, "..") {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	dir := filepath.Join(h.ThumbDir, hash)
	entries, err := os.ReadDir(dir)
	if err != nil {
		writeJSON(w, 200, []string{})
		return
	}

	var thumbs []string
	for _, e := range entries {
		if !e.IsDir() && strings.HasSuffix(e.Name(), ".jpg") {
			thumbs = append(thumbs, fmt.Sprintf("/thumbs/%s/%s", hash, e.Name()))
		}
	}

	writeJSON(w, 200, thumbs)
}
```

## static/js/app.js

```javascript
// === State ===
let allVideos = [];
let selectedHashes = new Set();
let thumbCache = {}; // hash -> [url, url, ...]
let thumbIntervals = {}; // hash -> interval ID

// === API Helpers ===
async function api(url, options = {}) {
    const resp = await fetch(url, {
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        ...options,
    });
    return resp.json();
}

// === Video Loading ===
async function loadVideos(query = '', tags = '') {
    const grid = document.getElementById('videoGrid');
    if (!grid) return;

    grid.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Loading videos</div>';

    let url = '/api/videos';
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    if (query) params.set('q', query);
    if (tags) params.set('tags', tags);
    if (params.toString()) url += '?' + params.toString();

    try {
        allVideos = await api(url);
        if (!allVideos) allVideos = [];
        renderVideoGrid(allVideos);
    } catch (err) {
        grid.innerHTML = `<div class="loading">Error loading videos: ${err.message}</div>`;
    }
}

function renderVideoGrid(videos) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('videoGrid');
    if (!grid) return;

    // Clear old thumb intervals
    Object.values(thumbIntervals).forEach(clearInterval);
    thumbIntervals = {};

    if (!videos || videos.length === 0) {
        grid.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">No videos found</div>';
        return;
    }

    grid.innerHTML = videos.map(v => {
        const thumbUrl = v.thumb_count > 0
            ? `/thumbs/${v.hash}/thumb_00.jpg`
            : '';
        const duration = formatDuration(v.duration);
        const tagsHtml = (v.tags || []).slice(0, 5)
            .map(t => `<span class="mini-tag">${escapeHtml(t)}</span>`)
            .join('');

        return `
            <div class="video-card" data-hash="${v.hash}" id="card-${v.hash}">
                <input type="checkbox" class="select-checkbox"
                       onclick="event.stopPropagation(); toggleSelect('${v.hash}')"
                       ${selectedHashes.has(v.hash) ? 'checked' : ''}>
                <div class="thumb-container"
                     onmouseenter="startThumbCycle('${v.hash}')"
                     onmouseleave="stopThumbCycle('${v.hash}')"
                     onclick="window.location='/video/${v.hash}'">
                    ${thumbUrl
                        ? `<img id="thumb-${v.hash}" src="${thumbUrl}" alt="" loading="lazy">`
                        : `<div style="position:absolute;top:50%;left:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);color:#666">No thumbnail</div>`
                    }
                    <span class="duration-badge">${duration}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="card-body" onclick="window.location='/video/${v.hash}'">
                    <div class="card-title" title="${escapeHtml(v.filename)}">${escapeHtml(v.filename)}</div>
                    <div class="card-meta">${escapeHtml(v.directory)}</div>
                    ${tagsHtml ? `<div class="card-tags">${tagsHtml}</div>` : ''}
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }).join('');
}

// === Thumbnail Cycling ===
async function loadThumbs(hash) {
    if (thumbCache[hash]) return thumbCache[hash];
    try {
        const thumbs = await api(`/api/thumbs/${hash}`);
        thumbCache[hash] = thumbs || [];
        return thumbCache[hash];
    } catch {
        thumbCache[hash] = [];
        return [];
    }
}

async function startThumbCycle(hash) {
    const thumbs = await loadThumbs(hash);
    if (thumbs.length <= 1) return;

    const img = document.getElementById(`thumb-${hash}`);
    if (!img) return;

    let idx = 0;
    thumbIntervals[hash] = setInterval(() => {
        idx = (idx + 1) % thumbs.length;
        img.src = thumbs[idx];
    }, 500);
}

function stopThumbCycle(hash) {
    if (thumbIntervals[hash]) {
        clearInterval(thumbIntervals[hash]);
        delete thumbIntervals[hash];
    }
    // Reset to first thumb
    const img = document.getElementById(`thumb-${hash}`);
    if (img && thumbCache[hash] && thumbCache[hash].length > 0) {
        img.src = thumbCache[hash][0];
    }
}

// === Search ===
function doSearch() {
    const query = document.getElementById('searchInput')?.value.trim() || '';
    const tags = document.getElementById('tagSearch')?.value.trim() || '';
    loadVideos(query, tags);
}

function clearSearch() {
    const si = document.getElementById('searchInput');
    const ts = document.getElementById('tagSearch');
    if (si) si.value = '';
    if (ts) ts.value = '';
    loadVideos();
}

// === Selection & Bulk Tagging ===
function toggleSelect(hash) {
    if (selectedHashes.has(hash)) {
        selectedHashes.delete(hash);
        document.getElementById(`card-${hash}`)?.classList.remove('selected');
    } else {
        selectedHashes.add(hash);
        document.getElementById(`card-${hash}`)?.classList.add('selected');
    }
    updateBulkBar();
}

function updateBulkBar() {
    const bar = document.getElementById('bulkBar');
    const count = document.getElementById('selectedCount');
    if (!bar || !count) return;

    count.textContent = selectedHashes.size;
    if (selectedHashes.size > 0) {
        bar.classList.remove('hidden');
    } else {
        bar.classList.add('hidden');
    }
}

function clearSelection() {
    selectedHashes.forEach(hash => {
        document.getElementById(`card-${hash}`)?.classList.remove('selected');
        const cb = document.querySelector(`#card-${hash} .select-checkbox`);
        if (cb) cb.checked = false;
    });
    selectedHashes.clear();
    updateBulkBar();
}

async function bulkAddTags() {
    const input = document.getElementById('bulkTagInput');
    if (!input) return;
    const tags = input.value.split(',').map(t => t.trim()).filter(t => t);
    if (tags.length === 0 || selectedHashes.size === 0) return;

    await api('/api/bulk/tags', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify({
            hashes: Array.from(selectedHashes),
            tags: tags,
            action: 'add'
        })
    });

    input.value = '';
    clearSelection();
    doSearch(); // Refresh
}

async function bulkRemoveTags() {
    const input = document.getElementById('bulkTagInput');
    if (!input) return;
    const tags = input.value.split(',').map(t => t.trim()).filter(t => t);
    if (tags.length === 0 || selectedHashes.size === 0) return;

    await api('/api/bulk/tags', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify({
            hashes: Array.from(selectedHashes),
            tags: tags,
            action: 'remove'
        })
    });

    input.value = '';
    clearSelection();
    doSearch();
}

// === Single Video Tag Editing ===
async function addTagsToVideo() {
    const input = document.getElementById('newTagInput');
    if (!input || typeof currentHash === 'undefined') return;

    const tags = input.value.split(',').map(t => t.trim()).filter(t => t);
    if (tags.length === 0) return;

    const video = await api(`/api/videos/${currentHash}/tags`, {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify({ tags })
    });

    input.value = '';
    renderTagContainer(video.tags || []);
}

async function removeTag(hash, tag) {
    const video = await api(`/api/videos/${hash}/tags`, {
        method: 'DELETE',
        body: JSON.stringify({ tags: [tag] })
    });

    renderTagContainer(video.tags || []);
}

function renderTagContainer(tags) {
    const container = document.getElementById('tagContainer');
    if (!container || typeof currentHash === 'undefined') return;

    container.innerHTML = tags.map(t =>
        `<span class="tag" data-tag="${escapeHtml(t)}">
            ${escapeHtml(t)}
            <button class="tag-remove" onclick="removeTag('${currentHash}', '${escapeHtml(t)}')">&times;</button>
        </span>`
    ).join('');

    // Reload similar videos
    if (tags.length > 0) {
        loadSimilarVideos(currentHash, tags);
    }
}

// === Similar Videos ===
async function loadSimilarVideos(hash, tags) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('similarGrid');
    if (!grid || !tags || tags.length === 0) return;

    // Search for videos with any of the same tags
    // We'll fetch all videos for each tag and merge
    let similarSet = new Map();

    for (const tag of tags) {
        try {
            const videos = await api(`/api/videos?tags=${encodeURIComponent(tag)}`);
            if (videos) {
                videos.forEach(v => {
                    if (v.hash !== hash && !similarSet.has(v.hash)) {
                        // Score by number of shared tags
                        const shared = (v.tags || []).filter(t => tags.includes(t)).length;
                        similarSet.set(v.hash, { video: v, score: shared });
                    }
                });
            }
        } catch (e) {
            // ignore
        }
    }

    // Sort by shared tag count descending
    let similar = Array.from(similarSet.values())
        .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
        .slice(0, 12)
        .map(s => s.video);

    if (similar.length === 0) {
        grid.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--text-muted)">No similar videos found</div>';
        return;
    }

    grid.innerHTML = similar.map(v => {
        const thumbUrl = v.thumb_count > 0 ? `/thumbs/${v.hash}/thumb_00.jpg` : '';
        return `
            <div class="video-card" onclick="window.location='/video/${v.hash}'">
                <div class="thumb-container">
                    ${thumbUrl
                        ? `<img src="${thumbUrl}" alt="" loading="lazy">`
                        : `<div style="position:absolute;top:50%;left:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);color:#666">No thumb</div>`
                    }
                    <span class="duration-badge">${formatDuration(v.duration)}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="card-body">
                    <div class="card-title">${escapeHtml(v.filename)}</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }).join('');
}

// === Tags Page ===
async function loadTagList() {
    const container = document.getElementById('tagList');
    if (!container) return;

    const tags = await api('/api/tags');
    if (!tags || tags.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">No tags yet</div>';
        return;
    }

    container.innerHTML = tags.map(t =>
        `<a href="/?tags=${encodeURIComponent(t.name)}" class="tag-item">
            ${escapeHtml(t.name)}
            <span class="tag-count">${t.count}</span>
        </a>`
    ).join('');
}

// === Utilities ===
function formatDuration(seconds) {
    if (!seconds || seconds <= 0) return '--:--';
    const h = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
    const m = Math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60);
    const s = Math.floor(seconds % 60);
    if (h > 0) {
        return `${h}:${m.toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${s.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
    }
    return `${m}:${s.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
}

function escapeHtml(str) {
    if (!str) return '';
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = str;
    return div.innerHTML;
}

// Handle tag links from tags page -> index page
(function() {
    if (window.location.pathname === '/') {
        const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const tags = params.get('tags');
        if (tags) {
            const tagInput = document.getElementById('tagSearch');
            if (tagInput) {
                tagInput.value = tags;
            }
            // Load with tags after DOM is ready
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => loadVideos('', tags));
            } else {
                loadVideos('', tags);
            }
        }
    }
})();
```

## main.go

```go
package main

import (
	"flag"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"

	"videolib/db"
	"videolib/handlers"
	"videolib/scanner"
)

func main() {
	// Command-line flags
	addr := flag.String("addr", ":8080", "Listen address")
	dbPath := flag.String("db", "videolib.db", "Database file path")
	thumbDir := flag.String("thumbs", "thumbnails", "Thumbnail directory")
	scanFlag := flag.Bool("scan", false, "Scan for new/deleted videos and exit")
	scanAndServe := flag.Bool("scan-and-serve", false, "Scan then start server")
	dirs := flag.String("dirs", "", "Comma-separated directories to scan for videos")

	flag.Parse()

	// Also accept directories as positional arguments
	scanDirs := flag.Args()
	if *dirs != "" {
		for _, d := range strings.Split(*dirs, ",") {
			d = strings.TrimSpace(d)
			if d != "" {
				scanDirs = append(scanDirs, d)
			}
		}
	}

	if len(scanDirs) == 0 {
		fmt.Println("Usage: videolib [flags] <directory> [<directory> ...]")
		fmt.Println()
		fmt.Println("Flags:")
		flag.PrintDefaults()
		fmt.Println()
		fmt.Println("Examples:")
		fmt.Println("  videolib --scan /path/to/videos")
		fmt.Println("  videolib --scan-and-serve /path/to/videos /other/videos")
		fmt.Println("  videolib /path/to/videos  # just serve (DB must exist)")
		os.Exit(1)
	}

	// Resolve absolute paths
	for i, d := range scanDirs {
		abs, err := filepath.Abs(d)
		if err != nil {
			log.Fatalf("Cannot resolve path %s: %v", d, err)
		}
		scanDirs[i] = abs
	}

	// Create thumbnail directory
	if err := os.MkdirAll(*thumbDir, 0755); err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Cannot create thumbnail directory: %v", err)
	}

	absThumbDir, _ := filepath.Abs(*thumbDir)

	// Open database
	database, err := db.Open(*dbPath)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Cannot open database: %v", err)
	}
	defer database.Close()

	// Handle scan mode
	if *scanFlag || *scanAndServe {
		s := scanner.New(database, scanDirs, absThumbDir)
		result, err := s.Scan()
		if err != nil {
			log.Fatalf("Scan failed: %v", err)
		}
		log.Printf("Scan complete: %d added, %d removed, %d errors, %d total on disk",
			result.Added, result.Removed, result.Errors, result.Total)

		if *scanFlag {
			return // Exit after scan
		}
	}

	// Start web server
	startServer(*addr, database, absThumbDir)
}

func startServer(addr string, database *db.Database, thumbDir string) {
	mux := http.NewServeMux()

	// API handlers
	apiHandler := handlers.NewAPIHandler(database)
	mux.HandleFunc("GET /api/videos", apiHandler.ListVideos)
	mux.HandleFunc("GET /api/videos/{hash}", apiHandler.GetVideo)
	mux.HandleFunc("POST /api/videos/{hash}/tags", apiHandler.AddTags)
	mux.HandleFunc("PUT /api/videos/{hash}/tags", apiHandler.SetTags)
	mux.HandleFunc("DELETE /api/videos/{hash}/tags", apiHandler.RemoveTags)
	mux.HandleFunc("POST /api/bulk/tags", apiHandler.BulkTags)
	mux.HandleFunc("GET /api/tags", apiHandler.ListTags)

	// Thumbnail API
	thumbListHandler := &handlers.ThumbListHandler{ThumbDir: thumbDir}
	mux.Handle("GET /api/thumbs/{hash}", thumbListHandler)

	// Media file serving (video files)
	videoHandler := handlers.NewVideoFileHandler(database)
	mux.Handle("GET /media/{hash}", videoHandler)

	// Thumbnail file serving
	thumbHandler := handlers.NewThumbHandler(thumbDir)
	mux.Handle("GET /thumbs/{hash}/{filename}", thumbHandler)

	// Static files
	staticDir := getStaticDir()
	mux.Handle("GET /static/", http.StripPrefix("/static/", http.FileServer(http.Dir(staticDir))))

	// Page handlers
	templateDir := getTemplateDir()
	pageHandler, err := handlers.NewPageHandler(database, templateDir)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Cannot load templates: %v", err)
	}
	mux.HandleFunc("GET /video/{hash}", pageHandler.VideoPage)
	mux.HandleFunc("GET /tags", pageHandler.TagsPage)
	mux.HandleFunc("GET /", pageHandler.Index)

	log.Printf("Starting server on %s", addr)
	if err := http.ListenAndServe(addr, mux); err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Server error: %v", err)
	}
}

// getStaticDir finds the static directory relative to the executable or CWD
func getStaticDir() string {
	// Try relative to CWD first
	if info, err := os.Stat("static"); err == nil && info.IsDir() {
		return "static"
	}
	// Try relative to executable
	if exe, err := os.Executable(); err == nil {
		dir := filepath.Join(filepath.Dir(exe), "static")
		if info, err := os.Stat(dir); err == nil && info.IsDir() {
			return dir
		}
	}
	return "static"
}

func getTemplateDir() string {
	if info, err := os.Stat("templates"); err == nil && info.IsDir() {
		return "templates"
	}
	if exe, err := os.Executable(); err == nil {
		dir := filepath.Join(filepath.Dir(exe), "templates")
		if info, err := os.Stat(dir); err == nil && info.IsDir() {
			return dir
		}
	}
	return "templates"
}
```

---

## Build & Run

```bash
# Initialize module
cd videolib
go mod init videolib
go mod tidy

# Build
go build -o videolib .

# First run - scan a directory of videos
./videolib --scan-and-serve /path/to/your/videos

# Subsequent runs - just serve (add --scan to update)
./videolib /path/to/your/videos

# Rescan to pick up new files
./videolib --scan /path/to/your/videos

# Then serve
./videolib /path/to/your/videos
```

## Prerequisites

**ffmpeg/ffprobe** must be installed for metadata extraction and thumbnail generation:

```bash
# Ubuntu/Debian
sudo apt install ffmpeg

# macOS
brew install ffmpeg

# Arch
sudo pacman -S ffmpeg
```

---

## Architecture Summary

| Component | Role |
|-----------|------|
| **BoltDB** | Single-file embedded DB with buckets for videos, path→hash index, tag→hashes index |
| **Hasher** | SHA-256 of first 10MB + file size to identify videos by content |
| **Scanner** | Walks directories, hashes files, probes with ffprobe, generates thumbnails via ffmpeg |
| **API** | REST endpoints for CRUD on videos/tags, bulk operations, search |
| **Pages** | Server-rendered HTML shells, data populated via JS calling the API |
| **Thumbnails** | 16 evenly-spaced JPGs per video; mouse-over cycles through them at 500ms intervals |
| **Bulk tagging** | Checkbox selection on grid → bulk add/remove tags to multiple videos at once |
| **Similar videos** | Shown under the player, ranked by shared tag count |

### Key design decisions:

- **Hash-based identity**: Videos are identified by a partial content hash (first 10MB + file size), so renaming/moving a file doesn't lose its tags — a rescan will match it by hash
- **Path index**: Fast lookup from filesystem path to hash, used during scanning to detect new/deleted files
- **Tag index**: Inverted index from tag → list of hashes for fast tag-based search
- **No transcoding**: Videos served directly via `http.ServeFile` which handles range requests (seeking) properly
- **Go 1.22 routing**: Uses the new `mux.HandleFunc("GET /path/{param}", ...)` pattern matching

## handlers/static.go (fixed)

```go
package handlers

import (
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"

	"videolib/db"
)

// VideoFileHandler serves the actual video files.
// It maps /media/{hash} to the actual file path from the database.
type VideoFileHandler struct {
	DB *db.Database
}

func NewVideoFileHandler(database *db.Database) *VideoFileHandler {
	return &VideoFileHandler{DB: database}
}

func (h *VideoFileHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	video, err := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	if err != nil {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	// Verify file still exists
	if _, err := os.Stat(video.Path); os.IsNotExist(err) {
		http.Error(w, "Video file not found on disk", 404)
		return
	}

	// Set content type based on extension
	ext := strings.ToLower(filepath.Ext(video.Path))
	contentTypes := map[string]string{
		".mp4":  "video/mp4",
		".webm": "video/webm",
		".ogv":  "video/ogg",
		".mkv":  "video/x-matroska",
		".avi":  "video/x-msvideo",
		".mov":  "video/quicktime",
		".wmv":  "video/x-ms-wmv",
		".flv":  "video/x-flv",
		".m4v":  "video/mp4",
		".ts":   "video/mp2t",
	}
	if ct, ok := contentTypes[ext]; ok {
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", ct)
	}

	http.ServeFile(w, r, video.Path)
}

// ThumbHandler serves thumbnail images
type ThumbHandler struct {
	ThumbDir string
}

func NewThumbHandler(thumbDir string) *ThumbHandler {
	return &ThumbHandler{ThumbDir: thumbDir}
}

func (h *ThumbHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	filename := r.PathValue("filename")

	if hash == "" || filename == "" {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	if strings.Contains(hash, "..") || strings.Contains(filename, "..") {
		http.Error(w, "Invalid path", 400)
		return
	}

	path := filepath.Join(h.ThumbDir, hash, filename)
	if _, err := os.Stat(path); os.IsNotExist(err) {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	w.Header().Set("Cache-Control", "public, max-age=86400")
	http.ServeFile(w, r, path)
}

// ThumbListHandler returns the list of thumbnail filenames for a video
type ThumbListHandler struct {
	ThumbDir string
}

func (h *ThumbListHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	if hash == "" || strings.Contains(hash, "..") {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}

	dir := filepath.Join(h.ThumbDir, hash)
	entries, err := os.ReadDir(dir)
	if err != nil {
		writeJSON(w, 200, []string{})
		return
	}

	var thumbs []string
	for _, e := range entries {
		if !e.IsDir() && strings.HasSuffix(e.Name(), ".jpg") {
			thumbs = append(thumbs, fmt.Sprintf("/thumbs/%s/%s", hash, e.Name()))
		}
	}

	writeJSON(w, 200, thumbs)
}
```

## static/js/app.js (fixed)

```javascript
// === State ===
let allVideos = [];
let selectedHashes = new Set();
let thumbCache = {};
let thumbIntervals = {};

// === API Helpers ===
async function api(url, options = {}) {
    const headers = {};
    if (options.body) {
        headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
    }
    const resp = await fetch(url, {
        headers,
        ...options,
    });
    if (!resp.ok) {
        throw new Error(`API error: ${resp.status}`);
    }
    return resp.json();
}

// === Video Loading ===
async function loadVideos(query, tags) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('videoGrid');
    if (!grid) return;

    grid.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Loading videos</div>';

    let url = '/api/videos';
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    if (query) params.set('q', query);
    if (tags) params.set('tags', tags);
    const qs = params.toString();
    if (qs) url += '?' + qs;

    try {
        const data = await api(url);
        allVideos = data || [];
        renderVideoGrid(allVideos);
    } catch (err) {
        grid.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Error loading videos: ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</div>';
    }
}

function renderVideoGrid(videos) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('videoGrid');
    if (!grid) return;

    // Clear old thumb intervals
    Object.keys(thumbIntervals).forEach(hash => {
        clearInterval(thumbIntervals[hash]);
    });
    thumbIntervals = {};

    if (!videos || videos.length === 0) {
        grid.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">No videos found</div>';
        return;
    }

    grid.innerHTML = '';

    videos.forEach(v => {
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'video-card' + (selectedHashes.has(v.hash) ? ' selected' : '');
        card.id = 'card-' + v.hash;
        card.dataset.hash = v.hash;

        const hasThumb = v.thumb_count && v.thumb_count > 0;
        const thumbUrl = hasThumb ? '/thumbs/' + v.hash + '/thumb_00.jpg' : '';
        const duration = formatDuration(v.duration);

        let tagsHtml = '';
        if (v.tags && v.tags.length > 0) {
            tagsHtml = '<div class="card-tags">' +
                v.tags.slice(0, 5).map(t => '<span class="mini-tag">' + escapeHtml(t) + '</span>').join('') +
                '</div>';
        }

        let thumbContent;
        if (hasThumb) {
            thumbContent = '<img id="thumb-' + v.hash + '" src="' + thumbUrl + '" alt="" loading="lazy">';
        } else {
            thumbContent = '<div style="position:absolute;top:50%;left:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);color:#666">No thumbnail</div>';
        }

        card.innerHTML =
            '<input type="checkbox" class="select-checkbox" ' +
                (selectedHashes.has(v.hash) ? 'checked' : '') + '>' +
            '<div class="thumb-container">' +
                thumbContent +
                '<span class="duration-badge">' + duration + '</span>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="card-body">' +
                '<div class="card-title" title="' + escapeHtml(v.filename) + '">' + escapeHtml(v.filename) + '</div>' +
                '<div class="card-meta">' + escapeHtml(v.directory) + '</div>' +
                tagsHtml +
            '</div>';

        // Event: checkbox
        const checkbox = card.querySelector('.select-checkbox');
        checkbox.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            toggleSelect(v.hash);
        });

        // Event: thumb hover
        const thumbContainer = card.querySelector('.thumb-container');
        thumbContainer.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
            startThumbCycle(v.hash);
        });
        thumbContainer.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
            stopThumbCycle(v.hash);
        });

        // Event: click to navigate
        thumbContainer.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.location.href = '/video/' + v.hash;
        });

        const cardBody = card.querySelector('.card-body');
        cardBody.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.location.href = '/video/' + v.hash;
        });

        grid.appendChild(card);
    });
}

// === Thumbnail Cycling ===
async function loadThumbs(hash) {
    if (thumbCache[hash]) return thumbCache[hash];
    try {
        const thumbs = await api('/api/thumbs/' + hash);
        thumbCache[hash] = thumbs || [];
        return thumbCache[hash];
    } catch {
        thumbCache[hash] = [];
        return [];
    }
}

async function startThumbCycle(hash) {
    const thumbs = await loadThumbs(hash);
    if (thumbs.length <= 1) return;

    const img = document.getElementById('thumb-' + hash);
    if (!img) return;

    let idx = 0;
    thumbIntervals[hash] = setInterval(function() {
        idx = (idx + 1) % thumbs.length;
        img.src = thumbs[idx];
    }, 500);
}

function stopThumbCycle(hash) {
    if (thumbIntervals[hash]) {
        clearInterval(thumbIntervals[hash]);
        delete thumbIntervals[hash];
    }
    // Reset to first thumb
    const img = document.getElementById('thumb-' + hash);
    if (img && thumbCache[hash] && thumbCache[hash].length > 0) {
        img.src = thumbCache[hash][0];
    }
}

// === Search ===
function doSearch() {
    const query = document.getElementById('searchInput');
    const tags = document.getElementById('tagSearch');
    loadVideos(
        query ? query.value.trim() : '',
        tags ? tags.value.trim() : ''
    );
}

function clearSearch() {
    const si = document.getElementById('searchInput');
    const ts = document.getElementById('tagSearch');
    if (si) si.value = '';
    if (ts) ts.value = '';
    loadVideos();
}

// === Selection & Bulk Tagging ===
function toggleSelect(hash) {
    const card = document.getElementById('card-' + hash);
    const checkbox = card ? card.querySelector('.select-checkbox') : null;

    if (selectedHashes.has(hash)) {
        selectedHashes.delete(hash);
        if (card) card.classList.remove('selected');
        if (checkbox) checkbox.checked = false;
    } else {
        selectedHashes.add(hash);
        if (card) card.classList.add('selected');
        if (checkbox) checkbox.checked = true;
    }
    updateBulkBar();
}

function updateBulkBar() {
    const bar = document.getElementById('bulkBar');
    const count = document.getElementById('selectedCount');
    if (!bar || !count) return;

    count.textContent = selectedHashes.size;
    if (selectedHashes.size > 0) {
        bar.classList.remove('hidden');
    } else {
        bar.classList.add('hidden');
    }
}

function clearSelection() {
    selectedHashes.forEach(function(hash) {
        var card = document.getElementById('card-' + hash);
        if (card) {
            card.classList.remove('selected');
            var cb = card.querySelector('.select-checkbox');
            if (cb) cb.checked = false;
        }
    });
    selectedHashes.clear();
    updateBulkBar();
}

async function bulkAddTags() {
    const input = document.getElementById('bulkTagInput');
    if (!input) return;
    const tags = input.value.split(',').map(function(t) { return t.trim(); }).filter(function(t) { return t; });
    if (tags.length === 0 || selectedHashes.size === 0) return;

    try {
        await api('/api/bulk/tags', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify({
                hashes: Array.from(selectedHashes),
                tags: tags,
                action: 'add'
            })
        });
        input.value = '';
        clearSelection();
        doSearch();
    } catch (err) {
        alert('Error: ' + err.message);
    }
}

async function bulkRemoveTags() {
    const input = document.getElementById('bulkTagInput');
    if (!input) return;
    const tags = input.value.split(',').map(function(t) { return t.trim(); }).filter(function(t) { return t; });
    if (tags.length === 0 || selectedHashes.size === 0) return;

    try {
        await api('/api/bulk/tags', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify({
                hashes: Array.from(selectedHashes),
                tags: tags,
                action: 'remove'
            })
        });
        input.value = '';
        clearSelection();
        doSearch();
    } catch (err) {
        alert('Error: ' + err.message);
    }
}

// === Single Video Tag Editing ===
async function addTagsToVideo() {
    if (typeof currentHash === 'undefined' || !currentHash) return;
    const input = document.getElementById('newTagInput');
    if (!input) return;

    const tags = input.value.split(',').map(function(t) { return t.trim(); }).filter(function(t) { return t; });
    if (tags.length === 0) return;

    try {
        const video = await api('/api/videos/' + currentHash + '/tags', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify({ tags: tags })
        });
        input.value = '';
        renderTagContainer(video.tags || []);
    } catch (err) {
        alert('Error: ' + err.message);
    }
}

async function removeTag(hash, tag) {
    try {
        const video = await api('/api/videos/' + hash + '/tags', {
            method: 'DELETE',
            body: JSON.stringify({ tags: [tag] })
        });
        renderTagContainer(video.tags || []);
    } catch (err) {
        alert('Error: ' + err.message);
    }
}

function renderTagContainer(tags) {
    const container = document.getElementById('tagContainer');
    if (!container || typeof currentHash === 'undefined') return;

    container.innerHTML = '';
    tags.forEach(function(t) {
        const span = document.createElement('span');
        span.className = 'tag';
        span.dataset.tag = t;
        span.textContent = t + ' ';

        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.className = 'tag-remove';
        btn.innerHTML = '&times;';
        btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            removeTag(currentHash, t);
        });

        span.appendChild(btn);
        container.appendChild(span);
    });

    // Reload similar videos
    if (tags.length > 0) {
        loadSimilarVideos(currentHash, tags);
    } else {
        const grid = document.getElementById('similarGrid');
        if (grid) grid.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--text-muted)">Add tags to see similar videos</div>';
    }
}

// === Similar Videos ===
async function loadSimilarVideos(hash, tags) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('similarGrid');
    if (!grid || !tags || tags.length === 0) return;

    grid.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Finding similar</div>';

    // Collect videos that share any tag
    let similarMap = {};

    for (let i = 0; i < tags.length; i++) {
        try {
            const videos = await api('/api/videos?tags=' + encodeURIComponent(tags[i]));
            if (videos) {
                videos.forEach(function(v) {
                    if (v.hash !== hash) {
                        if (!similarMap[v.hash]) {
                            similarMap[v.hash] = { video: v, score: 0 };
                        }
                        similarMap[v.hash].score++;
                    }
                });
            }
        } catch (e) {
            // ignore individual tag search failures
        }
    }

    // Sort by shared tag count
    let similar = Object.values(similarMap)
        .sort(function(a, b) { return b.score - a.score; })
        .slice(0, 12)
        .map(function(s) { return s.video; });

    if (similar.length === 0) {
        grid.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--text-muted)">No similar videos found</div>';
        return;
    }

    grid.innerHTML = '';
    similar.forEach(function(v) {
        const hasThumb = v.thumb_count && v.thumb_count > 0;
        const thumbUrl = hasThumb ? '/thumbs/' + v.hash + '/thumb_00.jpg' : '';

        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'video-card';
        card.style.cursor = 'pointer';
        card.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.location.href = '/video/' + v.hash;
        });

        let thumbContent;
        if (hasThumb) {
            thumbContent = '<img src="' + thumbUrl + '" alt="" loading="lazy">';
        } else {
            thumbContent = '<div style="position:absolute;top:50%;left:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);color:#666">No thumb</div>';
        }

        card.innerHTML =
            '<div class="thumb-container">' +
                thumbContent +
                '<span class="duration-badge">' + formatDuration(v.duration) + '</span>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="card-body">' +
                '<div class="card-title">' + escapeHtml(v.filename) + '</div>' +
            '</div>';

        grid.appendChild(card);
    });
}

// === Tags Page ===
async function loadTagList() {
    const container = document.getElementById('tagList');
    if (!container) return;

    try {
        const tags = await api('/api/tags');
        if (!tags || tags.length === 0) {
            container.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">No tags yet</div>';
            return;
        }

        container.innerHTML = '';
        tags.forEach(function(t) {
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = '/?tags=' + encodeURIComponent(t.name);
            a.className = 'tag-item';
            a.innerHTML = escapeHtml(t.name) + ' <span class="tag-count">' + t.count + '</span>';
            container.appendChild(a);
        });
    } catch (err) {
        container.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Error loading tags</div>';
    }
}

// === Utilities ===
function formatDuration(seconds) {
    if (!seconds || seconds <= 0) return '--:--';
    var h = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
    var m = Math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60);
    var s = Math.floor(seconds % 60);
    if (h > 0) {
        return h + ':' + String(m).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(s).padStart(2, '0');
    }
    return m + ':' + String(s).padStart(2, '0');
}

function escapeHtml(str) {
    if (!str) return '';
    var div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = str;
    return div.innerHTML;
}

// === Init ===
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Index page: check for tag params in URL
    if (window.location.pathname === '/') {
        var params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        var tagsParam = params.get('tags');
        if (tagsParam) {
            var tagInput = document.getElementById('tagSearch');
            if (tagInput) tagInput.value = tagsParam;
            loadVideos('', tagsParam);
        } else {
            loadVideos();
        }
    }

    // Search enter-key handlers
    var searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
    if (searchInput) {
        searchInput.addEventListener('keyup', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') doSearch();
        });
    }
    var tagSearch = document.getElementById('tagSearch');
    if (tagSearch) {
        tagSearch.addEventListener('keyup', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') doSearch();
        });
    }
});
```

Key changes:

1. **Removed the IIFE** at the bottom that raced with `DOMContentLoaded` — consolidated all init into one `DOMContentLoaded` handler
2. **Removed inline `onclick`/`onmouseenter`** from template literals — used `addEventListener` on DOM elements instead (template literals with embedded quotes/hashes were breaking)
3. **Removed the duplicate `loadVideos()` call** from `index.html`'s inline script — the init in `app.js` now handles it

Also remove the duplicate init from the template:

The `/media/` 404 was likely from inline JS constructing a URL with an undefined variable inside a template literal. Building the DOM properly with `addEventListener` avoids all those escaping/scoping issues.

USER: similar error now: 
(index):71  GET http://192.168.25.1:8023/media/ 404 (Not Found)
I think the template doesn't match maybe for a URL without the video id after /media/
I'm currently simply requesting the "start page" of the application. According to the log, it "indexed" four test videos just fine. Also, thumbnails were created for all of them. I did not "look into" the bolt database but it is there.

ASSISTANT: You're right — the `GET /media/` (with no hash) is coming from the `<video>` element in `video.html`. The issue is that `video.html`'s `{{define "content"}}` block contains a `<video>` tag with `/media/{{.Hash}}`, and the **layout template is being parsed and somehow triggered**.

But wait — you're on the **index page** (`/`). There should be no `<video>` element. Let me look at the template structure more carefully.

**Found it.** The problem is how Go's `html/template` parses the templates. When you use `ParseGlob("*.html")`, all files are parsed together. The `index.html` and `video.html` both define a block called `content`. **The second definition overwrites the first.** So when the index page renders `layout`, it uses the `content` block from `video.html` (or whichever was parsed last), which contains `<source src="/media/{{.Hash}}">` — and since the index page passes `nil` data, `{{.Hash}}` is empty, resulting in `/media/`.

The fix is to **not use a shared `content` block name**, and instead render each page template directly:

## handlers/pages.go (updated)

```go
package handlers

import (
	"html/template"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"path/filepath"

	"videolib/db"
)

type PageHandler struct {
	DB        *db.Database
	Templates map[string]*template.Template
}

func NewPageHandler(database *db.Database, templateDir string) (*PageHandler, error) {
	funcMap := template.FuncMap{
		"join": func(s []string, sep string) string {
			result := ""
			for i, v := range s {
				if i > 0 {
					result += sep
				}
				result += v
			}
			return result
		},
	}

	// Parse each page template individually, each including layout
	layoutFile := filepath.Join(templateDir, "layout.html")
	pageFiles := []string{"index.html", "video.html", "tags.html"}

	templates := make(map[string]*template.Template)
	for _, page := range pageFiles {
		t, err := template.New("").Funcs(funcMap).ParseFiles(
			layoutFile,
			filepath.Join(templateDir, page),
		)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
		templates[page] = t
	}

	return &PageHandler{
		DB:        database,
		Templates: templates,
	}, nil
}

func (h *PageHandler) render(w http.ResponseWriter, name string, data interface{}) {
	t, ok := h.Templates[name]
	if !ok {
		log.Printf("Template not found: %s", name)
		http.Error(w, "Template not found", 500)
		return
	}
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/html; charset=utf-8")
	if err := t.ExecuteTemplate(w, name, data); err != nil {
		log.Printf("Template error rendering %s: %v", name, err)
		http.Error(w, "Template error", 500)
	}
}

func (h *PageHandler) Index(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.URL.Path != "/" {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}
	h.render(w, "index.html", nil)
}

func (h *PageHandler) VideoPage(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	hash := r.PathValue("hash")
	video, err := h.DB.GetVideo(hash)
	if err != nil {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}
	h.render(w, "video.html", video)
}

func (h *PageHandler) TagsPage(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	h.render(w, "tags.html", nil)
}
```

The root cause: `ParseGlob` merged all templates into one namespace, so two `{{define "content"}}` blocks collided, and the video page's content (with its `/media/{{.Hash}}`) won the collision and rendered on every page with nil data.
